	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Cambridgeshire Guided Busway</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p class="mw-empty-elt">

</p>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><caption>Cambridgeshire Guided Busway</caption><tbody><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><a href="/wiki/File:TheBuswayLogo.svg" class="image"><img during trials, 2009</div></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;background-color: #efefef;">Overview</th></tr><tr><th scope="row">Owner</th><td><a busway</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Website</th><td><span class="url"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.thebusway.info/">www<wbr />.thebusway<wbr />.info</a></span></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;background-color: #efefef;">Operation</th></tr><tr><th scope="row">Began operation</th><td>7 August 2011</td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Operator(s)</th><td><a href="/wiki/Stagecoach_in_Huntingdonshire" class="mw-redirect" title="Stagecoach in Huntingdonshire">Stagecoach in Huntingdonshire</a>, <a href="/wiki/Go_Whippet" title="Go Whippet">Go Whippet</a></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;background-color: #efefef;">Technical</th></tr><tr><th scope="row">System length</th><td>16 miles (25&#160;km)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The <b>Cambridgeshire Guided Busway</b>, known locally as <b>The Busway</b>, connects <a href="/wiki/Cambridge" title="Cambridge">Cambridge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Huntingdon" title="Huntingdon">Huntingdon</a> and <a href="/wiki/St_Ives,_Cambridgeshire" title="St Ives, Cambridgeshire">St Ives</a> in the English county of <a href="/wiki/Cambridgeshire" title="Cambridgeshire">Cambridgeshire</a>. It is the longest <a href="/wiki/Guided_bus" title="Guided bus">guided busway</a> in the world,<sup id="cite_ref-bbcopens_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcopens-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bbcopening_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcopening-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> overtaking the <a href="/wiki/O-Bahn_Busway" title="O-Bahn Busway">O-Bahn Busway</a> in Adelaide, South Australia.<sup id="cite_ref-briefing_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-briefing-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-length_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-length-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Two guided sections make up 16 miles (25&#160;km) of the route. The northern section, which uses the course of the former <a href="/wiki/Cambridge_and_Huntingdon_railway" class="mw-redirect" title="Cambridge and Huntingdon railway">Cambridge and Huntingdon railway</a>, runs through the former stations of <a href="/wiki/Oakington_railway_station" title="Oakington railway station">Oakington</a>, <a href="/wiki/Long_Stanton_railway_station" title="Long Stanton railway station">Long Stanton</a> and <a href="/wiki/Histon_railway_station" title="Histon railway station">Histon</a>. The southern section, which uses part of the former <a href="/wiki/Varsity_Line" title="Varsity Line">Varsity Line</a> to Oxford, links <a href="/wiki/Cambridge_railway_station" title="Cambridge railway station">Cambridge railway station</a>, <a href="/wiki/Addenbrooke%27s_Hospital" title="Addenbrooke&#39;s Hospital">Addenbrooke's Hospital</a> and the park and ride site at <a href="/wiki/Trumpington,_Cambridgeshire" class="mw-redirect" title="Trumpington, Cambridgeshire">Trumpington</a>, via housing on the <a href="/wiki/Great_Kneighton" title="Great Kneighton">Clay Farm</a> site.
</p><p>Services are operated by <a href="/wiki/Stagecoach_in_Huntingdonshire" class="mw-redirect" title="Stagecoach in Huntingdonshire">Stagecoach in Huntingdonshire</a> and <a href="/wiki/Whippet_Coaches" class="mw-redirect" title="Whippet Coaches">Whippet Coaches</a>, which have exclusive use of the route for five years in exchange for providing a minimum service frequency between 07:00 and 19:00 each week day.<sup id="cite_ref-bbc-questions_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbc-questions-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Specially adapted <a href="/wiki/Bus" title="Bus">buses</a> are used: the <a href="/wiki/Bus_driver" title="Bus driver">bus driver</a> does not need to hold the <a href="/wiki/Steering_wheel" title="Steering wheel">steering wheel</a> on the guided sections of the busway. A total of 2,500,000 trips were made in the first year of operation.
</p><p>Proposed initially in the 2001 Cambridge-Huntingdon Multi-Modal Study, which recommended widening of the <a href="/wiki/A14_road_(England)" title="A14 road (England)">A14 road</a> and construction of a guided busway along the old railway lines, construction began in March 2007 and it was opened on 7 August 2011 after a succession of delays and <a href="/wiki/Cost_overrun" title="Cost overrun">cost overruns</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcopening_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcopening-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The original cost estimate of £116&#160;million rose to £181&#160;million by December 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> An independent review of the project was announced on 21 September 2010,<sup id="cite_ref-cn-independent-review_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cn-independent-review-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-hp-independent-review_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hp-independent-review-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> in which the Cambridge <a href="/wiki/Member_of_Parliament#United_Kingdom" class="mw-redirect" title="Member of Parliament">MP</a> <a href="/wiki/Julian_Huppert" title="Julian Huppert">Julian Huppert</a> at the time described the busway as a "<a href="/wiki/White_elephant" title="White elephant">white elephant</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> A court case with <a href="/wiki/BAM_Nuttall" title="BAM Nuttall">BAM Nuttall</a>, the main contractor, was settled by <a href="/wiki/Cambridgeshire_County_Council" title="Cambridgeshire County Council">Cambridgeshire County Council</a> in August 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Overview">Overview</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cambridgeshire_Guided_Busway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Overview">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The scheme links <a href="/wiki/Cambridge" title="Cambridge">Cambridge</a>, in East Anglia, with <a href="/wiki/St_Ives,_Cambridgeshire" title="St Ives, Cambridgeshire">St Ives</a>, <a href="/wiki/Huntingdon" title="Huntingdon">Huntingdon</a> and <a href="/wiki/Northstowe" title="Northstowe">Northstowe</a> (a proposed <a href="/wiki/New_town" class="mw-redirect" title="New town">new town</a>) to the north-west, and with the <a href="/wiki/M11_motorway" title="M11 motorway">M11 motorway</a> to the south. The route includes two sections of guided operation, a bus-only road and other places with on-street operation in conventional <a href="/wiki/Bus_lanes" class="mw-redirect" title="Bus lanes">bus lanes</a>. New <a href="/wiki/Park_and_ride" title="Park and ride">park and ride</a> sites have been built at <a href="/wiki/Longstanton" title="Longstanton">Longstanton</a> and at St Ives, with a tarmac cycle track/bridleway alongside some sections of the route.<sup id="cite_ref-bbc-questions_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbc-questions-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> The final scheme includes <a href="/wiki/Bus_priority" title="Bus priority">bus priority</a> and real-time <a href="/wiki/Passenger_information_system" title="Passenger information system">passenger information system</a> displays at busway bus stops; and subsequent separate funding and works to better link those stops to local businesses for pedestrians and cyclists.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A total of 2,500,000 trips were made in the first year of operation, which Atkins reported was 40% higher than the predicted figure. Bus use along the corridor was estimated to have increased by 33% over the same period.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Before opening, the contractor had predicted that an estimated 11,500 journeys per day would be made on the busway.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
The scheme was predicted to cause a direct reduction in traffic on the busy parallel <a href="/wiki/A14_road_(Great_Britain)" class="mw-redirect" title="A14 road (Great Britain)">A14 road</a> of 5.6% (rising to 11.1% with the new Park &amp; Ride sites), although as other traffic re-routes to the freed-up road space from other parts of the local road network, the net reduction is predicted to be 2.3%. The overall scheme was "not intended to solve the congestion problems on the A14" by itself, but will rather have an overall effect across the local road network, and be complementary to planned improvements on the A14.<sup id="cite_ref-DFTrep7_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DFTrep7-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Route">Route</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cambridgeshire_Guided_Busway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Route">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

</td></tr>
<tr>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<td class="RMl" colspan="2">
</td>
<td class="RMl1">
</td>
<td class="RMir"><div class="RM_"></div><div class="RM_"></div><div class="RM_"></div><div><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/BSicon_RP2q.svg/20px-BSicon_RP2q.svg.png" decoding="async" title="RP2q" width="20" height="20" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/BSicon_RP2q.svg/30px-BSicon_RP2q.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/BSicon_RP2q.svg/40px-BSicon_RP2q.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="500" data-file-height="500" /></div>
